** Sum function 'E' with plan('sequential') ...
function (...) 
{
    message("Arguments '...' exists: ", exists("...", inherits = TRUE))
    globals <- globals::globalsByName("...", envir = environment())
    f <- future({
        fcn <- function() sum(...)
        fcn()
    }, envir = parent.frame(), globals = globals)
    y <- value(f)
